57// apply a 3x2 matrix to a 2D color.
58pub fn spectrum_apply_3x2(matrix: [f64; 6], src: [f64; 2], tgt: &mut [f64; 2]) {
59    tgt[0] = matrix[0] * src[0] + matrix[1] * src[1] + matrix[2];
60    tgt[1] = matrix[3] * src[0] + matrix[4] * src[1] + matrix[5];
61}
62
63// Concrete conversion routines.
64pub fn spectrum_xy_to_xystar(xy: [f64; 2], xystar: &mut [f64; 2]) {
65    spectrum_apply_3x2(spectrum_mat_xy_to_xystar, xy, xystar);
66}
67pub fn spectrum_xystar_to_xy(xystar: [f64; 2], xy: &mut [f64; 2]) {
68    spectrum_apply_3x2(spectrum_mat_xystar_to_xy, xystar, xy);
69}
70pub fn spectrum_xy_to_uv(xy: [f64; 2], uv: &mut [f64; 2]) {
71    spectrum_apply_3x2(spectrum_mat_xy_to_uv, xy, uv);
72}
73pub fn spectrum_uv_to_xy(uv: [f64; 2], xy: &mut [f64; 2]) {
74    spectrum_apply_3x2(spectrum_mat_uv_to_xy, uv, xy);
75}

144pub fn xyz_from_spectrum(spectrum: &[f64; spectrum_num_samples], xyz: &mut [f64; 3]) {
145    *xyz = [0.0, 0.0, 0.0];
146    for i in 0..spectrum_num_samples {
147        xyz[0] += spectrum[i] * cmf_x[i];
148        xyz[1] += spectrum[i] * cmf_y[i];
149        xyz[2] += spectrum[i] * cmf_z[i];
150    }
151    xyz[0] *= spectrum_bin_size;
152    xyz[1] *= spectrum_bin_size;
153    xyz[2] *= spectrum_bin_size;
154}
155
156// This is 1 over the integral over either CMF.
157// Spectra can be mapped so that xyz=(1,1,1) is converted to constant 1 by
158// dividing by this value. This is important for valid reflectances.
159pub const equal_energy_reflectance: f64 = 0.009358239977091027;
